Special Article

Report on the Progress of Shanghai's First Literacy Schools

— Wu Tiecheng

In order to eliminate illiteracy and improve cultural standards in this city, special literacy education has been promoted. After several discussions on the preparations and points to note before implementation, these items have been separately disclosed and explained in the Shanghai Literacy Education Committee's Compilation of Programs and Regulations and in the Shanghai Literacy Education Special Issue of the Educational Magazine, Volume 25, No. 8, published by the Commercial Press. Since the promotion began, the first session has been completed, and the second session began teaching on September 5. In order to review the past and promote the future, the following is a general description of the progress of the first underground session.

I. Teaching Situation

The first session of municipal literacy schools, excluding the rural areas where they were not held due to the busy farming season, consisted of 220 schools in 19 districts. The number of schools were as follows: Temple District Office School, 20 schools in the Yimiao District, 20 schools in the Zhonghua District, 20 schools in the Gaochang District, 20 schools in the Qiu Bao District, 21 schools in the Datong District, 15 schools in the Qi Mei District, 14 schools in the Fahua District, 10 schools in the Pusong District, 10 schools in the Yangjing District, 10 schools in the Yinxiang District, 2 schools in the Yangsi District, 1 school in the Pu District, No schools were held in Zhenru, and 6 schools in the Caojing District. All of the above schools started on July 1 and ended on August 31, for a total of two full months. The final examinations were held on September 2. Of these, Caojing and Jiangwan districts each closed schools due to factual relations, so the actual number of completed schools was 218. The 200 literacy school teachers who passed the examination and completed three weeks of training, and the 20 selected from the Jiangwan Wenmiao Two Experimental Areas, totaled 220. Each teacher strove to teach with a spirit of hard work and endurance. However, more than ten people who were found to be perfunctory and incompetent were dismissed. This is why literacy education emphasizes strict rewards and punishments. The total number of students enrolled at the beginning of the first week was 54,541, of which adults accounted for about two-thirds and children accounted for about one-third. Adults were taught for one hour a day and graduated in February. Children were taught for one hour a day and graduated in April. During the session, according to the regulations of the Municipal Literacy School Chapter, those who taught for two hours a day graduated in one month, accounting for more than nine-tenths of the students. Only two or three schools still taught for one hour a day and had to wait until the next session to graduate. Textbooks were divided into two types for children and adults. Children's classes used the abridged short-term primary school textbook compiled by the Ministry of Education, divided into two volumes, one volume every two months. Adult classes used the Citizen Literacy Reader compiled by the Municipal Literacy Education Committee, also divided into two volumes, one volume per month. The total number of books issued to adults and children in the first session was 469,500 (including books used by private literacy schools and educational service groups; there are also cases where books were received but not used up and have not yet been returned). The average number of classes per school was five (including one children's class) or four (including two children's classes). There were very few schools with only four adult classes. The average number of students per class was about 50. The total number of classes in the city was 1,014. Teachers in the first session did not take holidays, so 22 substitute affairs staff were set up, averaging one per ten schools. Due to the number of schools set up in each district in the first session, the number of staff allocated could not be one per district, so some districts had several staff members, or several districts shared one. The allocation was determined and each district had a table showing which school and which day the substitute teacher would be teaching, so that the teachers could be reassigned. However, there were also temporary allocations. The number of schools, classes, and enrolled students in each district are shown in the table below at the beginning of the session. However, two or three weeks after the start of classes, some students requested to join, and some requested to change the date, so the number of students in the table differs from the number of students in the final examination results. (To be continued)

Recreation Special

Painless Quitting of Opium?

— Dun Gen

People who quit opium are most afraid of pain. They initially took it up to avoid the pain of illness, and now they desperately want to quit, but their mouths cannot stand the pain: (1) the pain of old illnesses recurring, (2) the pain of new illnesses increasing (such as back pain, leg weakness, back spasms, stomach pain, abdominal pain, dry mouth, dry throat, liver fire, red eyes, tearing, runny nose, yawning, coughing, extreme sweating, hot flashes, nocturnal emission, diarrhea, insomnia, irritability, etc. caused by quitting opium), (3) doctors who are inexperienced, inconsiderate, use insufficient medication, or perform surgery awkwardly, especially injections and blister extraction.

There are too many speculative doctors in the market who all claim to offer "painless opium quitting." Unfortunately, the three words "painless opium" have been abused to the point of discrediting. Now, let's take blister extraction as an example: Since a certain general called a foreign doctor to use blister extraction injections to quit opium, it became fashionable in Shanghai for a time. All doctors touted blister extraction as fashionable and flaunted their skills. No matter how skillful they are, I'm afraid that "blister extraction" is not painless. I have a wealthy friend who went to a certain hospital to quit opium. He stayed in a first-class ward, and the doctor fawned on him. The doctor performed blister extraction for him, applying a medicine to his chest. After a day and a night, a large yellow blister formed. He said that he could hardly bear the pain during that day and night, just like the old method of mashing garlic and applying it to break the skin and cause blisters. The doctor comforted him, telling him to sleep peacefully and forget the pain. But how could he sleep or forget? When the blisters were fully formed, the yellow water was extracted with an empty needle and re-injected into the blood vessels. After two more painful extractions and injections, it was over. He still talked about it afterward with lingering pain. He also said that he still had cravings after the water extraction injection. As long as he drank less of the craving suppressant, he still felt weak until two months later, when the main ingredient of the suppressant was completely eliminated and he had eaten a lot of tonics, he finally succeeded. So I know that quitting opium requires a gradual reduction method. Water extraction injection is indeed a newly invented medical technique, but to be completely painless and to quit completely in three or four days without any other aids and never relapse, I'm afraid it's not something everyone can do. (Before egg yolk essence became popular, many people who used the water extraction injection method to quit opium also relied on tonic injections for at least a week to resist mental fatigue.) Today, I sincerely advise my fellow compatriots who are determined to quit opium that if you want a stable, safe, and painless method, you should still use the "gradual reduction" method while taking egg yolk essence as an aid. This method cannot be better! Because after taking egg yolk essence, you can reduce the amount of opium by two-tenths every four or five days. In the end, to be more stable, reduce from two-tenths to one-tenth, from one-tenth to five-hundredths, from five-hundredths to two and a half-hundredths, and from then on until you completely stop smoking (those who swallow bubbles, eat earth, or inject morphine can also use this reduction method). Although some people may feel physically weak, they can inject egg yolk essence for one or two weeks. The egg yolk essence injection is not very painful when injected, but it's like being bitten by a mosquito. However, the pain of water extraction injections is greater. Everyone! I am not a doctor and am not soliciting opium-quitting business. These words are honest, fair, and unbiased. Because I am considerate of the physical weakness, fear of pain, and preference for gradual quitting among my fellow opium-quitting compatriots, I am contributing these experiences. If you can start taking egg yolk essence and reducing your opium consumption today, you can still catch up with quitting within the year and avoid the lack of freedom of government-mandated opium quitting.

Anecdotes about Opium

— Jiang Deqi

Guo Jifen's Laughingstock

During the Qing Dynasty's Guangxu reign, Guo Jifen was awaiting assignment as a circuit intendant in Zhejiang. He once served as the director-general of the Wenzhou-Chu Salt and Tax Bureau. Because he collected less than the quota and owed arrears, he was impeached and dismissed. Zeng Zigu, the governor of Zhejiang, investigated and found that the shortfall was due to weather conditions and the arrears were due to manpower constraints. He deemed the situation justifiable and reinstated him. However, after only a year, Zeng impeached him again for opium use, and he was stripped of his post. When Guo entered the opium prohibition center for examination, he placed a large plaster on his anus. The plaster was opium paste, not medicine. According to custom, officials entering the examination center had to exchange all their clothing, shoes, socks, and even belts for government-owned items, from head to toe. When Guo changed his pants, the committee member saw the plaster on his anus and asked about it. Guo said that it was used to treat hemorrhoids. The committee member removed it and examined it, saying, "This looks like opium paste. It should be kept for examination." Guo strongly protested. The committee member had no choice but to let him keep it on, but closely monitored his movements. However, since the opium paste had been applied to hemorrhoids, it was too dirty to be ingested. The legal deadline was one week. On the second day, Guo could no longer bear it and begged the monitor to allow him to swallow opium pills, promising to keep the secret and offering a reward of ten thousand gold. The committee member reported the situation to the director-general. Guo's plan failed. He confessed to smoking opium and was released that day. The director-general reported to the governor, who, according to regulations, decided to strip him of his post.

The Xianfeng Emperor's Opium Addiction

During the Qing Dynasty's Xianfeng reign, the prohibition of opium gradually relaxed. Many high officials at that time were addicted to it. Even the emperor himself was fond of this substance. When the Anglo-French Allied Forces entered Beijing, the emperor fled north to Rehe. In addition to his fear and anxiety, his addiction kicked in, leading to a serious illness. At that time, the emperor was forced to flee because he had taken opium with him. The emperor was also angry that the Opium War had led to foreign troops invading. He deeply regretted succumbing to its poison, so he decided to quit. Unexpectedly, this led to his illness. Alas, the poison of opium is painful throughout the world, and even the emperor of the time destroyed his life with it. How painful it is!

Exquisite Couplets

My hometown scholar, Pan Kaisheng, was unrestrained in his literary talent and did not engage in farming. He was deeply addicted to opium. He once wrote two couplets that are still recited by the villagers as conversation starters. One reads: "When will the mouth blowing a flute without holes attract a phoenix?" "The hand holding a bald brush scribbles all day long." The other reads: "The lamplight is not as good as the starlight, but it can still shoot at the Big Dipper." "Foreign medicine is not the same as gunpowder, but it can also fire a gun."

Occasional Opium Couplets

— Er Xi

I enjoy collecting satirical couplets in my spare time. I have already collected many. I have now extracted a few that satirize the fun of smoking opium to share with my fellow literati to bring some joy.

(1) There is a couplet imitating the Yunnan Daguanlou couplet, satirizing opium smokers: "Five hundred taels of opium mud borrowed into the hand, cheap and pure, joyfully and endlessly. Look at Guangdong boasting black soil, Hubei valuing red gelatin, Guizhou valuing green mountains, Yunnan valuing white water, assessing the colors and distinguishing them, and inviting guests to comment leisurely. Taking advantage of the fire being strong and the stove being hot, the fish roe and crab eye are boiled, just dreading the long night, so arrange some snowy jade peaches to avoid wasting the four-sided censer, the ten thousand character incense tray, the nine-sectioned old gun, and the three-xiang jade mouthpiece. Thousands of taels of family property are forgotten, and the mind is exhausted, laughing at how useful endless wealth is. Think of the famous Bakhus, the precious Fushou, the Cheng-passed poppy, and the flower named hibiscus. Lying with a lit lamp, enjoying all the pleasures of life, just smoking morning and night, not afraid of the scorching sun and cold tides, even if the wife complains and the children cry, just pretend to be deaf and dumb, only leaving a few inches of prisoner hair, half a shoulder, two lines of tears, and a dry skeleton."

(2) There is a couplet that imitates the City God Temple couplet to create a couplet for opium dens: "No matter how lawless you are, when you get here, can you still be strong?" "You must know that I don't lend or owe, so put down your afraid guns and count the money quickly."

(3) A scholar had an opium addiction and once made a couplet to satirize himself: "One couch is laid out, never mind the earth cracking, the sky collapsing, the sea drying, and the stones rotting." "Half a lifetime is wasted, there will always be a day when the smoke dissipates, the fire goes out, the oil is exhausted, and the lamp dries up."

(4) There is a couplet satirizing those who set up lamps in ancestral halls to sell opium: "Breathing in sync with the ancestors is the true line of incense." "Laughing at descendants who haven't read poetry and books but know the lamps and fire at the third watch."

(5) There is a couplet created by collecting phrases for opium dens: "Heavy curtains don't roll up, leaving fragrance for a long time," "Short flute has no tune, blowing as you please."

(6) Another couplet satirizes smokers: "Without system, holding up the mourning stick early, before death, lighting the upside-down lamp first."

Song Submissions

The Evils of Opium (An Imitation of New Suzhou Ballads)

— Yu Mengjiang

Speaking of opium, it's so harmful... Oh dear, it harms us common people, making us poor and weak, it's truly hateful! Ever since it spread until now, it's been the main reason for the nation's crisis! The Qing Dynasty produced Lin Zexu, who wanted to ban opium! He said that... If opium is prevalent for ten years, the country will have nowhere to find silver for the military, and if it spreads for a hundred years, the country will have no soldiers to use. Those hateful British people started a war, drawing swords and spears. We can only hate Empress Dowager Cixi and Li Hongzhang, who were weak, incompetent, and afraid of war, and could only cede territory and pay compensation, signing unequal treaties. This is the root of the disaster of national subjugation and annihilation. Think about whether you hate it or not... hate. (Passing through the door)

Some people say that it's okay for rich people to smoke... as long as they can afford some fake foreign snacks, fine paste, large soil, and white bronze lamps. When collecting the paste, they use ginseng, and beautiful wives and concubines serve them, exhaling clouds and spitting mist, turning into immortals. But once you enter this city of hibiscus, sweetness turns into bitterness later on. Spending two taels is a small matter, as weakness and illness follow one after another. Today they invite a doctor, tomorrow they need a morphine shot. They pick and choose doctors to do more business... (Passing through the door)

You must know that opium contains morphine, which can only temporarily excite you. For a while, it's truly like an immortal's joy, but over time, it will turn into a disease. You become confused and disoriented day and night, and constipation is extremely painful. My parents gave me this six-foot body, but I become disabled for life, which is truly pitiful. Perhaps all kinds of careers will collapse in an instant, or perhaps all the wealth will be swallowed in one gulp... (Passing through the door)

I insist on saying that it's even more pitiful for poor people to smoke... wasting time and losing their jobs, spending their days in vain. The ancients said: "An inch of time is worth an inch of gold, but an inch of gold cannot buy an inch of time!" Isn't it true that great times are wasted for a lifetime? Some suffer from great economic oppression, and their wives and children are separated, which is very heartbreaking. The whole family runs away, and relatives and friends don't recognize them. They can only go to the swallow's nest to be coolies. If they miss a dose for a day, their defenses are down, and they'll see King Yama from typhoid fever. After they die, they'll be buried in the countryside. Think about whether it's pitiful or not... pitiful. (Passing through the door)

Today, I advise you gentlemen and friends... whether you are poor, rich, or businessmen, in short, if you smoke opium, you should quit as soon as possible. Now there is a kind of "Kang Le Su" (Health and Happiness Element), formulated with scientific methods, containing lecithin, which is nutritious and warm. As long as you buy and take it for a month, I guarantee you'll quit and be at peace. From then on, all misfortunes will be eliminated, and you can live happily ever after...

Ten Exhortations (Yangzhou Tune: Dressing Table)

— Feng Danxia

First exhortation. First, I exhort farmers. Exhort the farmers. Quit opium. Revive your spirits. Our China. Originally is. Based on agriculture. All farmer friends. On both shoulders. Responsibility is not light. Calloused hands and feet. Spring plowing and summer weeding. You must know. Food on the plate. Every grain is hard-earned. Both quit smoking and quit planting. Eradicate poisonous plants. Only then am I worthy of being a good farmer in China. Second exhortation. Again, I exhort all laborers. Your position. Second only to agriculture. Rely on both hands. Exchange for money. Maintain life. Why bother. Turn your blood and sweat. Squander it on wine and opium. Work after smoking. Strive to study books. Seek knowledge. And skills. Increasingly proficient. Rely on thought. And ingenuity. Invent new objects. Only then. Can you be worthy of. Labor heroes. Third exhortation. Third, I exhort all merchants. The merchant's position. Rising like the sun. World trade show. Competition is fierce. Prepare. Good skills. Compete for this win or lose. Make a profit on the capital. Speculate and calculate the win. Business development. All rely on faith and sincerity. Donate huge sums. Help military use. Receive awards. (Recently, the newspaper reported that Mr. Bei Runsheng was commended by the National Government for helping Mr. Chen Yingshi with 100,000 yuan in military supplies) Such a merchant. His name will last forever.

Fourth exhortation. Respectfully exhort you gentlemen in the academic world. Your knowledge. Not as good as blindly. Teachers are solid, predecessors are aware. Numerous students. Also future owners. Essence and virtue. Transforming rain and spring breeze. Never. Smoke opium. Tarnish in the school. The ancients said. A gentleman's fault. Like a solar eclipse. Get central village. And educate. Its joy is harmonious.

Fifth exhortation. Deeply exhort soldiers. Secure the country and resist foreign aggression. The responsibility is heavy and unparalleled. Tiger head and ape arms, the appearance of being enfeoffed as a marquis. Never. Smoke opium. Destroy your own Great Wall. Hear the rooster and dance with the sword. Throw the pen and ask for a ribbon. To achieve meritorious service in foreign lands. Bronze pillars inscribed with merit. Rely on your head. And blood. Avenge the country. Drink the Yellow Dragon wine heartily. Sweep the cave and plow the courtyard.

Sixth exhortation. Gently exhort you honorable officials. Your position. How superior and honorable. Alert in advance. Observe afterwards. Secure the good and eliminate the violence. Sleepless and restless. The mouth does not speak of merit. People's hearts are like their faces. Each is different. Inevitably there are "hidden dragons" among them. I advise you to quickly leave the cave of smoke and mist. So that you can avoid. To be criticized by others. Attacked by ten thousand mouths.

Seventh exhortation. Sincerely exhort you scholar-officials. Learning is excellent. Ancient and modern are the same. Now officials are called servants. Four hundred million. Master. What are you waiting for. Bright and decisive. Benevolent and forgiving. Never. Smoke opium. Enter the wrong path. If you have it, change it, if you don't have it, encourage yourself. Suddenly repent. Naturally. Wash away the filth of the old dyes.

Eighth exhortation. Advise the rich. Now money. Known as omnipotent. Since it is called omnipotent. The path must be carefully considered. Why. Waste useful. Most of it is burned on the fire. This quickly quit opium. Save the poor. Plant blessings. Reap good fruits. Not a hair's breadth. Luxurious seats and thick shoes. How many lives have you cultivated? Hungry without food. Cold without clothes. The same is born of heaven. Ninth exhortation. Bitterly exhort the poor. I am a child. And you. The same is precarious. Seeking clothing and food. Already not easy. How can you smoke opium. Enter hell yourself. Resolve to quit addiction. Be determined not to waver. When misfortune reaches its limit, prosperity will come. The peeling and restoration omen is the first. Ancient and modern heroes. Many years out in the cold gate. Don't. Love black smoke. Endlessly fascinated.

Tenth exhortation. Universally exhort you compatriots. The painful history of opium. My clumsy pen can hardly describe. Hundreds of years of loss. Wonderful calculations are difficult to audit. Only fall to. People are poor and the country is weak. The wind and rain are swaying. The government decided on a major plan. Four years limited is not far. From now on. The pipe and stove will be extinguished and the smoke will disappear. Even more thanks to that. Doctor Tang. Invented "Kang Le Su". I wish you compatriots to ascend to "Kang Le". Enjoy the joy.

— Ba Weng

The harm of opium is known to everyone. Now, imitating Liu Yuxi's "Inscription for a Humble Room," I jokingly wrote an "Inscription for a Smoking Room" to warn those who are addicted to opium.

The area is no longer large. Famous people come out. The paste is not much. It's not good if you don't come. This is a smoking room. Only without moral fragrance. Poem Modification

— Shou Ju

There was a family in Taizhou with six or seven brothers who all had close relations with the poppy. Over the years, their essence and blood and the wealth of their family were all sucked dry by the poppy, turning them into nothing. I jokingly modified an ancient poem to sing about it: "Going two, three forward. Four, five opium lamps. Six, seven brothers. Eighty, ninety guns." (Note: The ancient poem is "Going two, three li. Four, five houses in the village ahead. Six, seven pavilions. Eighty, ninety flowers." It is a sentence from a red tracing book used by children to practice writing in the old days.)

Important Announcement Regarding Kang Le Su

Kang Le Su is a type packaged in glutinous rice hulls. (That is, the box is packed. Each box contains twenty pieces.) In the summer season. Because the climate is humid. As a result, the oil exudes outside the shell. When swallowing, it is held in the mouth with warm water. It is not easy to soften for a while. Distributors in various places are slightly careless in storage. Even moldy. Now it's better. The weather is dry. The shells are white and oil-free. It is easy to dissolve in water. Those who buy and take it all praise it. Inland areas willing to be distributors. Quickly come to purchase and promote it. Wealthy families. You can buy a few more boxes with confidence. Avoid the trouble of buying in small quantities. You can also get a bargain. Isn't that great?

Sports News

Mr. Hu Wenhu Leads the Powerful Overseas Chinese Troops from Malaya, Arriving Today

The ships will dock at the China Merchants Bureau's North Wharf at 3 PM. Representatives from various groups will gather at the port to welcome them. It is also scheduled to hold a tea party at the Great Shanghai Garden on the 7th.

The athletes from the Malayan Chinese community who participated in the 6th National Games, led by general team leader Hu Wenhu and Lin Aimin, arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning on the Italian postal ship Conte Verde. They are scheduled to arrive at the port at 3 PM today and dock at the China Merchants Bureau's North Wharf on East Broadway Road. Various groups in the city have decided to prepare a grand welcome and held the first preparatory meeting at the YMCA in Baxianqiao at 4 PM yesterday to discuss welcome methods. Details are recorded below:

Groups Attending: The groups attending yesterday included the Bureau of Education, the Bureau of Social Affairs, the Chinese Aviation Association, the Shanghai Sports Advancement Association, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Fujian Association in Shanghai, the Shanghai Vagrant Learning Institute, the Shanghai National Products Factory Union, the Huangshan Construction Committee, the Shanghai Relief Association for Flood Victims in Various Provinces, Zhahe Middle School, Guanshengyuan, and other institutions and groups. Representatives Nie Haifan, Hu Zongfan, Peng Quji, Li Dachao, Hu Guigeng, Zhu Boyuan, Huang Bodu, Li Chenmian, Wei Langxuan, Zheng Jie, Sun Choucheng, Yuan Zengyu, Wu Tang, Li Wenbin, and others attended.

Chairman's Report: Chairman Li Dachao first gave a report, stating that the Preparatory Committee had properly handled matters concerning pier order, the Public Security Bureau's band, Boy Scouts, and team flags and symbols, and had obtained a permit from the Customs for a 40-person group to board the ship to welcome them upon arrival in Shanghai. The order of the welcome ceremony, the route for touring the city, and visits to local attractions had also been drafted and requested to be approved.

Mayor Sends Telegram to Welcome: Since yesterday afternoon, Hu Guigeng, manager of the Shanghai branch of Wing On Company, received a wireless telegram from Hu Wenhu from the ship, stating that he would arrive at the port at 3 PM tomorrow (today). Mayor Wu of the city and various groups in Shanghai sent telegrams to the ship to express their welcome. The original telegrams are recorded as follows: (1) Mayor Wu's telegram: "To Mr. Hu Wenhu and all athletes, we sincerely welcome you, Mayor Wu Tiecheng of Shanghai." (2) Telegram from various groups to the Conte Verde ship, delivered to Mr. Hu Wenhu: "We welcome you and all the athletes to Shanghai with the most sincere enthusiasm, Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education, Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and 95 other groups."

Telegram from Chen Guofu, Chairman of Jiangsu Province: "To Mr. Hu Guigeng of Tiger Brand Wing On Company, transferred to Mr. Hu Wenhu, I am very happy to hear that you are returning to Shanghai. I have specially sent Secretary Yao Dingchen to Shanghai to welcome you on behalf of my admiration. I hope you will take the time to visit Jinjiao's scenic spots to wash away the dust of Shanghai, Chen Guofu."

Key Resolutions: After discussion, it was resolved that the representatives of the welcoming groups should arrive at the China Merchants Bureau's North Wharf on East Broadway Road at 2 PM tomorrow (today) and disperse after the team leader and athletes land. (2) The representatives of the Preparatory Committee groups will bring three flower baskets and a list of the welcoming groups to board the ship to welcome them, and the entire group will take a photo. (3) Please send a large car from the municipal government to be led by the Preparatory Committee's team leader to the Liangjiang Women's Physical Education School. (4) All representatives of the Preparatory Committee groups should gather at the YMCA in Baxianqiao at half past noon tomorrow (today) to go to the pier. (5) It was decided to hold a preparatory meeting at the Great Shanghai Garden at 4 PM on the 6th.

Grand Welcome: The Preparatory Committee decided that after Hu and others arrive in Shanghai today, they will be tired from the journey, and they will rest for one day tomorrow (the 6th). At 3 PM on the 7th, a grand welcome tea party will be held at the Great Shanghai Garden, with performances by several famous movie stars and singers. The order is as follows: (1) Play music, (2) Pay the highest respect to the party flag, national flag, and the portrait of the Prime Minister, (3) Read the Prime Minister's will, (4) Silent meditation for one minute, (5) The presidium delivers a welcome speech, (6) Speeches, (7) The Malaysian Chinese team leader answers, (8) Photography, (9) Tea party, (10) Entertainment. All welcome invitations are being printed and distributed to all sectors.

Tour Route: The association rented 50 Xiang Sheng cars for the athletes to take a tour of the city and visit major factories and the battlefields of the Songhu War. The route is as follows: Starting from Liangjiang (the reception cars will gather at the YMCA in Baxianqiao and depart), go to the Confucian Temple Public Group in Nanshi, enter Manufacturing Bureau Road, visit the Jiangnan Shipyard and the Naval Aircraft Manufacturing Plant, turn north onto Zhejiang Road, walk on Nanjing Road, cross the Baidu Bridge eastward, North Suzhou Road, to the North Station, enter Baoshan Road to the north, see the Dongli Library and the site of the Commercial Press, pass through Tianyong'an and reach the city center via various circuits, tour the Municipal Government Building, and go to Shanghai Construction Chuangong Road Zao River, and visit the Wusong Fort. The meeting ends.

A Glimpse of Strength: The Malayan Chinese athletes participating in the National Games include men's and women's track and field, swimming, and ball sports, a total of five events. There are famous players such as Jin Cheng, Yang Anni, and Deng Yinjiao. The strength is very strong, and the football team is especially strong. It can compete with the strong teams from Guangdong, Hong Kong, and Shanghai. In track and field, Ye Suian's long jump of 7 meters is expected to break the national record. Jin Cheng's sprint is also outstanding. Deng Yinjiao's running and jumping have long been famous in the country. Ge Yulian's high jump of more than 1.30 meters is also commendable. It is a pity that the famous swimmers Chen Weishui and Yang Anni, the mermaid of the South Sea, who have repeatedly set national records, were unable to accompany them. Otherwise, they would not let Yang Weiqiong and others have all the glory. The men's tennis team has a high voice for the championship.

Football Performance: The Malaysian Chinese football team has many famous players such as Guan Shunde, Xie Qingfu, and Lin Yachi. The strength is strong, and they have a grand plan to annex the three Wu regions. It is hoped that the team will have the most hope. The team will rest in Shanghai and change to the 8th (originally scheduled for the 9th) at 2 PM in Shenyuan to play a performance match with the local emerging team of young footballers. At that time, the fans can enjoy the game. The full list of the team is as follows: Liu Jingu, Huang Jinbai, Lin Xifu, Chen Qiwan, Chen Yuanyun, Chen Yaning, Jian Erhui, Ji Youling, Lin Jinyun, Lin Ziquan, Lin Yachi, Yao Shenghua, Li Yiyou, Peng Jinqing, Xie Qingfu, Guan Shunde, Cai Qianan.

Overseas Chinese Tour: The Nanyang Overseas Chinese 6th National Games Observation Group, organized by the Youth Aspiration Society of Singapore, led by Lin Xinmin, also came to Shanghai on the same ship. In addition to visiting the National Games, they will also investigate the political, educational, economic, and social conditions of the city. The Municipal Bureau of Education has ordered the municipal social education institutions to facilitate this.

Education Bureau's Instructions: The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education issued instructions to public and private schools and social education institutions, stating, "According to the Municipal Government's Order No. 157000, it is opened within: 'According to the Consulate General in Penang, it is reported that the athletes from various regions of Malaya and China are all overseas Chinese children who have never been allowed to enter the country. Their concept of the motherland is inherently weak. They can take this opportunity to return to the country to participate in the National Games. In terms of sports, they can mutually learn from each other. At the same time, they can gain considerable knowledge and understanding of the political, educational, economic, and social conditions of the country. Strengthen the sincerity of the overseas Chinese to the interior and increase the national thinking of overseas Chinese students. If the organizing committee of the National Games can give guidance and liaison, and other institutions, schools, and groups can provide convenience for visits, the number of participating athletes from Malaya is more than 130, and their enthusiasm for the motherland is commendable. If the team needs to visit various institutions and schools after arriving in Shanghai, it should be given special convenience to show preferential treatment. In addition to distributing it to the organizing committee of the National Games, we should ask you to check and handle it.' etc. We hereby order you to comply with and order your subordinates to comply with it. This order.'"

Two to Zero, Sichuan Football Team Won Against South China Yesterday, Football Won, Basketball Lost

The Sichuan athletes have been in Shanghai for many days. They have been practicing hard for days. Yesterday, the football and basketball teams successively arranged matches with South China and Youyou. As a result, the football team won two to zero, and the basketball team lost forty-two to forty-five.

Football Team Wins Against South China

The Sichuan National Games football team lost to Guanghua in the previous game due to travel fatigue and unfamiliarity with the venue. Yesterday, they played a friendly match with South China at Shenyuan Stadium. Overall, the Sichuan team's skills have improved a lot. The internal guards are tightly guarded, and the cooperation of the five forwards is also good. As a result, the Sichuan team won two to zero. It is reported that the Sichuan team will also arrange a friendly match with the Youyou team next Monday. The battle situation yesterday is recorded on the right.

First Half: At 3 PM, the competition began. The Sichuan team's nine forwards advanced together. The ball was often in front of the South China team's goal. The Sichuan team shot many times, but none of them hit. South China counterattacked and knocked on the door twice, but also failed to score. From then on, the South China team declined. Later, Zeng Zhengqi of the Sichuan team got the ball, dribbled into the enemy's camp, passed it to Zhong Laijin, and with a strong kick, the ball entered the net. The first half ended with a score of one to zero.

Second Half: After changing sides, the ball was still in front of the South China team's goal. The Sichuan team shot several times, but failed to hit. In the last few minutes, Yun Chongqing of the Sichuan team snatched the enemy's ball and attacked the South China team directly. Yang Guisheng of the South team blocked, and Yun secretly passed to Zhou Tailin. Zhou passed it to Liu Yinming from afar, and Liu raised his foot and shot obliquely. The Sichuan team scored another goal. The overall result was two to zero. The lineups of both sides are as follows:

The National Games Preparatory Committee is Preparing to Grandly Welcome Lin and Wang to the Conference

Three thousand elementary school students will rehearse Tai Chi exercises today. All venues will be open from today for practice. The Railway Bureau has announced measures for referees and athletes' vehicles.

The 6th National Games, which is scheduled to open on the 10th of this month, is approaching soon. The Preparatory Committee has been quite busy recently. The progress of various items has been explored as follows:

Measures to Maintain Order at the Conference: The Preparatory Committee has finalized the order of the venues for the National Games. It is planned that the Security Department will allocate 500 police officers, and the Public Security Bureau's Police Training Institute will allocate 500 police officers, totaling 1,000, to maintain order together with the Boy Scouts of the city. The Police Training Institute has already allocated 150 police officers yesterday, led by Captain Wu, to be stationed at the main stadium.

Formal Banquet to Welcome Lin and Wang to Shanghai: Chairman Lin Sen of the National Government, President Wang Jingwei of the Executive Yuan, and others are all participating in the opening of the National Games and are scheduled to come to Shanghai on the day. The Preparatory Committee has decided on welcome measures. Large arches will be set up at the road ends around the venue, and a formal banquet will be held during the arrival of the two. President Wang replied to Mayor Wu yesterday that he would come to Shanghai on the 9th to participate in the opening of the National Games on the morning of the 10th. President Wang donated 200 yuan in his personal name for the travel expenses of the athletes from Qinghai who participated in the National Games, and also allocated 100 yuan to help the athletes from Nanjing, which was handed over to the two teams on the 3rd.

All Venues Will Be Open From Today

The venue equipment department of the National Games Committee, in view of the imminent opening of the National Games and the arrival of athletes from all over the country, has specially stipulated the opening hours of each venue for the athletes to practice in. All track and field venues, swimming pools, gymnasiums, football fields, and tennis courts will be open from today until the 8th. The opening hours of track and field venues and swimming pools are from 3 PM to 5 PM, football fields are from 4 PM, gymnasiums are from 7:40 AM to 5:40 PM, and tennis and volleyball courts are from 7:30 AM to 5:30 PM. The baseball and softball fields will be completed within a few days and will be open from the 7th to the 9th. The city's track and field team participating in the National Games is scheduled to hold a general practice at the venue at 3 PM tomorrow.

Today's Tai Chi Practice Rehearsal

Three thousand elementary school students from thirty-six schools in the city, participating in the National Games' Tai Chi performance, are scheduled to hold a general rehearsal at the National Games venue at 3:00 PM today. Mr. Chu Minyi has arrived in Shanghai and will personally direct the rehearsal. The original plan for the Education Bureau to arrange for vehicles to pick up students at seven designated locations has been changed to train transportation. The details are as follows: (1) For the general rehearsal, the Shanghai Education Bureau originally designated seven assembly points with vehicles provided for transportation. This method has been changed to train transportation. (1) Leaders and all children participating in the Tai Chi general rehearsal will all travel by train, in two separate trips. (A) Meeting Train: 1. The first train will depart from the South Station at 12:00 noon and Xujiahui at 12:10 PM, directly to the Sanmin Road Station at the venue. 2. The second train will depart from the North Station at 2:00 PM sharp, Tiantong'an Station at 2:05 PM, and Jiangwan Station at 2:13 PM. (B) Train from the venue to Shanghai: It will depart from Sanmin Road Station at 4:30 PM. Please note that those who arrived on the first train will be sent back first, followed by those who arrived on the second train. (1) Personnel from the China Travel Service will be stationed at each station to check the number of students arriving from each school together with the stationmaster. (1) Each school must adhere to the train schedule at each station and arrive early to wait; latecomers will not be accommodated. (1) When entering the station and boarding the train, form two vertical lines for counting. (1) Leaders and students must all wear Tai Chi uniforms. The first train will pick up students from the following schools (19 schools) at the South Station, totaling 1,600 people: Wanzhu, Yangzheng, Yangshangwen, Xicheng, Wuben, Shihua, Bide, Jingye, Yonghui, Nongtan, Nandang, Dongming, Minglun, Jiangjing, Meixi, Chongzheng, Shiji, Xunyu, and Deyuan. The train from Xujiahui will pick up one school, totaling 50 people. The second train will depart from the North Station, picking up (8 schools) totaling 700 people: He'an, Minzhi, Tongshan, Shanghai Elementary School, Shuji, Qingde, Feiyu, and Peiben. The train from Tiantong'an Station will pick up (6 schools) totaling 550 people: Yucai, Qimei, Haishan, Chengzhong, Ningbo No. 2 Elementary School, and Guangdong Elementary School. Qiujiang and Zhongshan. These thirty-six schools total 3,000 people.

Temporary Radio Station Begins Transmitting and Receiving

The Shanghai Telegraph Bureau of the Ministry of Communications, in light of the fact that the National Games is scheduled to open on October 10th, and to ensure the prompt transmission of various records to all parts of the country, has established a temporary telegraph receiving and transmitting station within the National Games venue. Equipped with the latest type of Creed high-speed automatic machine, the station has been fully set up and will be officially established and begin transmitting and receiving telegrams this morning. Personnel from the original receiving station in the city center will be transferred to serve at this location. After the National Games concludes, the original setup will be restored.

Transportation Arrangements for Referees and Athletes

The Two-Roads Administration received an order from the Ministry of Railways stating: "Approved per the Education Department's Document No. 12706 dated September 14th, regarding the National Games Preparatory Committee's forwarded lists of referees and athletes eligible for reduced or free transportation, along with sample credentials, please review and handle accordingly." Accompanying the request were 200 copies each of referee travel route tables and athlete participation route tables, as well as 500 each of free and reduced-fare transportation passes, and 200 sample copies of each type of credential. As such, the Games are being held in Shanghai, and athletes' travel should be eligible for the reduced-fare passes, charging a quarter of the ticket price upon presentation of the pass. Referees are specially permitted to use the free transportation passes, boarding the train directly with the free pass. Each free pass is limited to one person; multiple people cannot share a single pass. Furthermore, attention should be paid to the transportation instructions printed on the back of each pass, strictly enforcing them to prevent abuses. It is also essential to verify the names listed on the referee travel route tables and the phrase 'travel by Hu-Ping-Yong train' filled out in the athlete participation route tables for Anhui. However, travel on the Hu-Ping-Yong train should not be subject to reduced fares and should still require the purchase of full-price tickets. In addition to forwarding the original passes to the Education Department and sending separate telegrams, we are urgently enclosing 30 copies of each original table and 30 copies of each sample pass for your road to forward and strictly implement. Minister Gu Mengyu, Deputy Minister Zeng Shenming (acting) signed and sealed. The bureau has instructed the Transportation Department to comply accordingly.

Elementary School: Local Games and Mechanical Exercises

Compiled by Cai Yanbin, published by Qinfen Bookstore

Qinfen Bookstore, located at 392 Route Labourdonnais, Shanghai, has published over a hundred types of educational series, which have long been praised throughout the country. Now, the bookstore has published "Elementary School: Local Games and Mechanical Exercises," compiled by Cai Yanbin, director of physical education at the National Jiyi University Experimental Elementary School. The content is divided into two parts: local games and mechanical exercises, with a total of fifty teaching materials. It is suitable for elementary school students in the upper grades. The upper part includes thirty teaching materials such as planting watermelons, catching flowers, jumping stone steps, setting off small firecrackers, good friends, guessing games, dodging pats, and interlocking rings. The lower part includes twenty teaching materials such as front squat support, elbow support, half-rotation sedan, and raising left and right feet high. Each teaching material is interesting, and the compiler has been tested many years before editing. The whole book is priced at four corners, with a postage fee of nine cents for mail orders from outside the city. The market department of Qinfen Bookstore at 27 Simada Road, Shanghai, is also distributing the book.

Fudan University 30th Anniversary

Celebration set for the 7th, 8th, and 9th of the month; Various departments to host exhibitions

Fudan University, located in Jiangwan, Shanghai, was founded seven years before the founding of the Republic of China and was the first school independently run by the Chinese people. It boasts a beautiful environment and has always been highly regarded. This year marks the 30th anniversary of its founding. The 7th, 8th, and 9th of October are designated as celebration dates, with various exhibitions and performances. There will be military and musical performances. The commemorative ceremony will be held at 3:00 PM on the 7th. The schedule for the three days is as follows: October 7th, exhibitions from 9:00 AM to 12:00 PM; military performances from 1:30 PM to 3:30 PM; a gathering parade at 3:30 PM; the 30th-anniversary ceremony from 4:00 PM to 6:00 PM; an alumni banquet at 7:00 PM; fireworks at 9:30 PM. October 8th, exhibitions from 9:00 AM to 11:00 AM; alumni and student sports competitions from 3:00 PM to 6:00 PM; a grand musical gathering from 7:30 PM to 11:00 PM. October 9th, exhibitions from 9:00 AM to 12:00 PM; Chinese martial arts performances and recreational sports from 3:00 PM to 5:30 PM; Peking opera from 7:00 PM to 11:00 PM. Alumni associations from various regions will send representatives to participate and gather for dinners and celebrations. Each department of the Colleges of Liberal Arts, Science, Law, and Business will hold large-scale exhibitions. The departments of Chinese, Foreign Languages, Education, and Sociology in the College of Liberal Arts will exhibit achievements in the form of photographs, charts, and graphs. The Department of Journalism will hold a world newspaper exhibition. The departments of Chemistry, Physics, Civil Engineering, and other departments in the College of Science will display models, specimens, and achievements. The various departments of the College of Law and Business will present statistical charts and tables for public reference.

Journalism Department to Hold Newspaper Exhibition, Review Daily

The Department of Journalism at the University plans to hold a world newspaper exhibition, soliciting newspapers from home and abroad, as well as printing and telecommunications machinery, statistical charts, etc., for public display for the reference of those concerned with journalism. It will open on the 7th of this month, with the exhibition divided into four parts. The materials in each part are extremely rich. "Domestic Newspapers": Newspapers sent for display come from eighteen provinces and eight cities. Newspapers from various border provinces are participating, totaling more than 1,200 copies. Major newspapers, small newspapers, city newspapers, and inland newspapers present a grand spectacle. In addition, there are 200 valuable compilation volumes of various newspapers and 50 special items of historical value, all of which are rare materials. Each newspaper is labeled with a small card, detailing information such as address, founding year, capital, and circulation. "Foreign Newspapers": The collection of foreign newspapers was facilitated by the assistance of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and the results are quite impressive. There are 38 participating units, including Europe, America, Asia, Australia, and the Philippines, covering five continents, including 26 independent countries and 12 colonies, with different languages, which is quite interesting. The newspaper masthead has a small card indicating the founding year, capital, circulation, and other information of the newspaper. In addition, advertising samples from the French "Petit Marseillais" newspaper, advertising paper from the New York "Biuchamtion" newspaper, and a sample of the first issue of the American "Sun" newspaper founded in 1833 are all rare materials. "Printing Machinery": The printing machinery exhibition includes a large flatbed press from the Laina Printing Machinery Factory, a new-style type-casting machine, a Laina typewriter, Lihe Foreign Firm's color printing machine, Tailai Foreign Firm's three-color printing machine, an automatic type-casting machine, Kongshi Foreign Firm's lead plate paper plate, Mingjing Machinery Factory's casting furnace, and a copper plate printing machine, all of which will be on-site for live demonstrations. Lida Foreign Firm, Lixing Ink, and Lian Ink, Chen Senji and Huafeng Type Foundry lead type copper molds, China Book Company's three-purpose copying machine, Telecommunications Machinery, China Electric Company has automatic telephone machines, switchboards, teletypewriters, various ammeters, measuring instruments, vacuum tubes, etc., Siemens Foreign Firm has telephone exchanges, international radio stations, and Shanghai Telegraph Bureau has telegraph receiving and sending machines. "Statistical Charts": In this section, in addition to dozens of statistical charts sent by Shen, Xin, and Shi newspapers, all framed and displayed, there are more than 200 volumes of communication drafts from various news agencies, working photos of various newspapers, and photos of martyrs in the journalistic field, a dazzling array.

Little Men (66)

— Original work by Ms. Alcott, translated by Zheng Xiaocang

Of course, there were no classes that morning, and by the afternoon, the damaged room had been cleaned up, and the patient was better, so there was time to calmly listen to and try those little criminals. Ned and Tommy had explained their part in the wrongdoing, regretting that they had brought their beloved home and those inside it to the brink of danger. But Don was still in that nonchalant, "who cares?" mood and was unwilling to admit how much damage had been done.

Mr. Bae hated nothing more than drinking, gambling, and swearing; even smoking cigarettes, he had given up himself, so that the children would not imitate him. Therefore, he was filled with anger and sorrow to see the boys, whom he had repeatedly treated with patience, taking advantage of his absence to introduce these forbidden evils, making his pure children think that such indulgence was heroic and refreshing. He gathered the children and gave them a detailed lecture, finally saying with a firm yet sympathetic expression:

"I think Tommy has suffered enough pain, and the scar on his arm will make him remember for a long time not to get involved in these things again. Ned's panic is enough for him, because he has already regretted it, and he can indeed listen to my instructions. But you, Don, I have forgiven you several times, and it has been of no use to you. I cannot let my children be corrupted by your bad example, nor do I want my time to be wasted in vain, saying things that are not accepted, so you can say goodbye to everyone, and ask Nasui to pack your things in my black bag.

Page 17

Spring and Autumn

Tidbits

— (Zheng Yimei)

Climbing high on the Double Ninth Festival has been a routine story for nearly several thousand years. Indeed, during the Double Ninth Festival, the sky is clear and the air is crisp. Invite three close friends, and leisurely walk up the green hills in the suburbs. The red maple leaves and the yellow chrysanthemums, reflecting each other, are worth stopping for everywhere, and enjoyable to appreciate everywhere. Occasionally pick dogwood flowers and casually wear them. The fragrance of dogwood and chrysanthemums, permeating the clothes, almost makes one forget all the troubles and worries of the world. On the way back, pass by a country inn, boldly enter, and sit behind the window overlooking the flowing water. Drink lightly and slowly, talking about the past and present, without any restraint or taboo. Drink until the crows return in the setting sun, and the darkening sky begins to appear, then each returns home slightly drunk. It can truly be said to be enjoying life in a timely manner. However, the origin of climbing high on the Double Ninth Festival, as recorded in the "Sequel to the Harmonious Records of Qi," says: "Fei Changfang ordered Huan Jing to carry dogwood flowers in a bag on the ninth day of the ninth month and climb high to avoid misfortune." It can be seen that this day was not entirely a day for joyful celebration. It was not until later, when the governor brought wine, and Meng Jia's hat fell off, that the original intention was deviated from, and this was used as an opportunity for autumn outings and banquets.

Someone said: "This year's floods, from summer to autumn, have affected a wide area. The Yangtze River flooded first, and then the Yellow River breached its banks. Fields and houses have been completely submerged. There is simply no place to live on the flat ground. People have flocked to the hills and forests to barely survive. This kind of disguised climbing high is indeed to avoid disasters, and one can deeply sympathize with the ancient person Huan Jing."

The same climbing high, we are so carefree and happy. Those who are avoiding disasters, have no home to return to, no work to do, and are starving and freezing to death, are so miserable and painful. So, how should we show compassion and kindness, and generously donate to provide relief?

The Hometown and Relics of Xi Shi

— Sun Linchang

Everyone knows that Xi Shi was an ancient beauty, but some people only know that she was lent by the King of Yue to seduce Wu, and then her fate is unknown. One saying is that Fan Li carried her away together, but in fact, she died to save her mother. Now, I have received a report from my old friend Mr. Feng, and I am writing about the hometown and relics of Xi Shi below. Mr. Feng is a native of Zhuji, so he has firsthand knowledge, and his words should be true.

The hometown of Xi Shi is Luoluo Village, located outside the South Gate of Zhuji County along the right bank of the Huansha River. There is a small hill, and going straight to the right, there is a wooden archway with the four characters "Ancient Luoluo Village" written on it. This is the entrance to the Xi Shi Temple. The temple is a two-room, one-courtyard hall facing north and south. In the middle is a niche with statues of Xi Shi and two palace maids. The four characters above the niche read "Committed to Other Ambitions." The statue of Xi Shi is in the center, holding a book, standing gracefully, looking very lifelike. On the side of the temple is the South Hall, with the inscription "Place of Returning to Truth," next to it is a couplet: "Entrusting the body to live by the Huan River, declaring the ambition to die for the river, returning to the sky in one death. Being pure in the mountains, still unpolluted when coming out of the mountains." "Obeying orders to enter Wu, succeeding in the mission and retreating to Yue, serving the old mother in the Five Lakes. Being filial to one's parents and showing loyalty to the country." There are two couplets in the temple corridor, one of which reads: "Born in the home of Xi Shi's maternal family, loyal to the former master, filial to parents, she is an unparalleled woman in China." "Caring about the overall situation of the Eastern Zhou Dynasty, seducing the powerful Wu, reviving the remnant Yue, she is truly the greatest person in the world." The other one says: "Don't say that Su Xiao of Qiantang is a fellow villager, please tell about her above." "Just call Xi Shi of Huansha River a beauty, how can one convey the truth." Behind the temple on the right is a small pond, with a stele that reads "Rouge Pond." Outside the temple, overlooking the opposite stream, bamboo fences and thatched houses, with trees forming forests, this is Xizi Village. It is said to be the former residence of Xi Shi. Along the stream across Hengtang, there is a pavilion, called "Huansha Pavilion," which is the place where Xi Shi threw herself into the river to save her mother.

The Origin of the Hairy Child

— Sun Choucheng

After reading the news in the third page of this newspaper on September 28, "Kuang Zhongmou Takes in a Hairy Child with Hair All Over His Body," driven by curiosity, I went to Penglai Market to visit Mr. Kuang. He kindly answered my questions about the process of taking in the child, which was more detailed than what was reported in the newspaper. Therefore, I am transcribing it below to supplement the deficiencies of the previous report. (The following is all from Mr. Kuang): The child was brought by magician Ma Shouyi when he performed at the Penglai Grand Theater in this market in August of this year. Mr. Ma has a long-standing reputation and has traveled extensively in Europe and the United States, with footprints all over the world. He has always been known as a strange talent, so everything he does is filled with strangeness. The child was born in Shaojiadaying, thirty miles north of Yingzhou, Anhui Province. His father's name is Shao Zhenquan, who is thirty years old this year, and his mother's name is Zhang, who is twenty-six years old. The family has been farming for generations, and the couple are simple and honest villagers. According to their own account, they had a son and a daughter. The son died young, and the daughter is already five years old. This child is the third child, born on the ninth day of the fifth lunar month last year, and is now fourteen full months old. At birth, there were no other abnormalities. The facial features and limbs were the same as ordinary people, and the physique was fat and radiant. The strange thing is that the skin is dark, the eyes are bright and shiny, and the whole body's hair is like a hedgehog, shining golden yellow. The hair on the face grows to several inches long, drooping like willow branches, incomparably soft, almost covering the face. The hair at the connection between the nostrils and the lips is particularly thick. The hair in the ear holes is even longer, fluffy like a tuft of hair, wrapped around the cheeks. The hair on the coccyx is dense and gradually forms the shape of a tail. This is only in terms of its external form. As for its special anomalies, one must visit in person to fully understand its bizarre and strange appearance, and sigh at the wonder of creatures in the world. When I (Mr. Kuang refers to himself) first saw the child, I thought it was made by artificial means. When I stroked his face, I realized that it was indeed natural. Because his hair grows on his cheeks, curly and shiny, resembling a lion, I temporarily named him "Lion-Shaped Hairy Little Man," which seems more accurate than the "Hairy Child" reported in the newspaper. I agreed to keep him in the Penglai Garden for public exhibition, for the appreciation and research of people from all walks of life. His parents are also protecting him by his side, and detailed inquiries can be made. However, the ignorant villagers believe that photography is ominous. Therefore, I have repeatedly tried to take photos to keep as a souvenir, but they have been rejected, and they said that if I want to take photos, I must guarantee that he will have no disasters or misfortunes, and no diseases within three years. The closed nature of the inland atmosphere can be seen from this. I hope that physiologists and eugenicists will personally visit, investigate and study, and publish the relationship between them, so that the strange is not separated from the proper, so that everyone's doubts can be relieved, and so that my good intention to take in the child will not be in vain.

Black Shadows Enshrouding Europe

The Lost Records of Imperial Incense

— By Princess Der Ling, translated by Qin Shouou

(Chapter Omitted) The Meeting of the Author and Translator

I casually asked if, after arriving in Peiping, you would be staying at the home of your younger sister, Mrs. Tang Binzhao! - Princess Rong - home. Unexpectedly, this sentence aroused her complaints. She said very indignantly:

"Rongling? We two don't get along! I can say that I have never corresponded with her, let alone stay at her house!"

This startled me. Sisters should be so close, and this older sister had been away from the country for so long. This time when they reunited, it should have been so happy! But unexpectedly, there was such a strange situation. From the look in her eyes, I could imagine that she would never talk to her sister after arriving in Peiping this time. I was a sincere friend, so I couldn't help but say many words to persuade her, and I also said how much her younger sister missed her. If she didn't object, I would be willing to send a telegram to ask Princess Rongling to meet her at the station.

"I don't want her to meet me!" Older people tend to be stubborn.

In fact, in "The Lost Records of Imperial Incense," she repeatedly mentioned "My Sister" and "Mysister," so she must have been very eager for this sister in her heart. It was because there may have been some misunderstanding at the beginning, so she was unwilling to soften her attitude. But as someone who doesn't have an older brother or a younger brother, I felt very sad.

Generally, when people talk about unpleasant events, it is difficult to continue the conversation. Moreover, seeing the look in her eyes, knowing that I had a good impression of Mrs. Tang, she suspected that I was on Mrs. Tang's side, so I could only force a smile and say nothing.

Because she was also someone who made a living by selling articles, we turned the conversation to talk about business matters. When she heard me say that every thousand words usually only sold for four, five, or six yuan, she smiled and said that that was only enough to buy jam. The value of her writing in the United States was calculated page by page with the bookstore owner after she finished writing a book, which was at least four or five times higher than ours.

The porters on the platform were shouting "Passengers seeing off the guests, please get off the train!" I asked her to sign her name on the back of my card. Unfortunately, she still signed in English. By the time I wanted to ask her to sign in Chinese, it was too late. I thought this was not important, and when she came back in two or three weeks, she could sign it again. What I was most concerned about was whether she could change her mind after arriving in Peiping and make peace with her sister (End).

Short Story

Mother

— Wu Yafei

Mother always coughed non-stop every night, and each time she coughed so hard, as if she couldn't catch her breath. It was really hard for me to hear. But after I repeatedly asked for her consent to ask a doctor to prescribe some medicine for her, I couldn't overcome her strong will. She often said to us:

"I can eat well, excrete well, and I'm not sick, so why see a doctor?" But she never finished more than two bowls of rice. Sometimes when she worked harder, she would even skip a meal or a day, which was common. But she wouldn't let go of her work, and she would still get up and do it.

"Mother, your constant coughing is very harmful to your body! Why don't you want to see a doctor?" This was my repeated plea after being rejected, but her fixed consciousness never wavered my sincere and passionate request.

"Coughing is an old illness, and seeing a doctor may not be effective. This illness was caused when I gave birth to you, and no one served me, so I went to the river to wash diapers and caught a cold. It's been almost decades now; what's the big deal about coughing..." Mother always explained the reason why she didn't want to take medicine in this way, but she just wanted to save us some money.

I had also tried several times to buy some tonics for her to eat, but she had been rejected by her stubbornness.

Mother was widowed early in life. There was no permanent property in the family, only three dilapidated yellow stone houses. There was no field, no land, only a few barren mountains. Moreover, when my father passed away, he left behind more than a thousand yuan of debt. The interest alone was one hundred and three yuan a year.

Debts had to be repaid, interest had to be paid, and me, my younger brother, and herself had to live. At this time, my younger brother was only four years old, and I was only nine years old. However, she didn't want us to be scavengers, so she sent both of us brothers to a village school to study. Where did this tuition fee come from? Did she not care? She had a strong will and a spirit of struggle. Therefore, she was not discouraged and never gave in, enduring the pain and struggling. She didn't need the help of relatives, and she didn't want to beg for help from clansmen. She only knew how to work hard, take the money she earned to pay off debts, provide for our lives, and give us education. Without complaints or sorrows, she believed that the future was full of light—only hoping that her two children would grow up, and everything would be fine, and everything could be solved, as long as we brothers worked hard and made progress.

Now, although ridicule, sarcasm, cruelty, and grief surrounded her, she was still very optimistic because us brothers were her only comfort. She often said to us in an encouraging tone:

"Children, study hard. Mom has worked so hard for you, hoping that you will make your dead grandmother and father proud. We don't need to be envious of those who have food and clothing. As long as you grow up, you will have everything." When she said this, her eyes were already a little wet, but she continued excitedly: "Because your grandmother was also widowed at the age of twenty-two, and only had your father. Now that your father has passed away so early, leaving you two children, this burden is on my shoulders..." Struggle

When we reached the age of fourteen, she had to ask people to help us find work. My body had been weak since I was a child, so I had to find something less strenuous. My younger brother was very strong, so it was no problem for him to work as a laborer. Before long, things were settled, so she was busy preparing bedding and luggage for us, and raising travel expenses, which was really painstaking.

After we finished our studies, because she saw that the dilapidated house was uninhabitable and very dangerous, she tried to build five new houses for us. She thought that with five houses, we two brothers would have enough to live in. But as soon as the new house was completed, she was anxious to have grandchildren, so she arranged my marriage. From then on, we owed more than two thousand yuan of debt. Moreover, with the recent rural bankruptcy, the debt only continued to increase. Therefore, she had to continue to work hard to help us. Because of this, she had to endure the wind and dew and run around even at this old age!

But what about us? It's a shame to say! I couldn't make her proud, and I increased her disappointment! Sorrow! Pain! Grief! Alas! This unfilial sin cannot be forgiven even if I am crushed to pieces!

Acknowledgement: The Yuanchang Advertising Company at No. 7 Sanrangfang, Caishi Road, Shanghai, recently published "Experiments and Discussions on Goldfish Breeding." The content is divided into fourteen sections, including the key to goldfish breeding and experience, which are concise and not empty talk. (Printed on gold paper and white paper, the special price is two cents per copy, and the postage stamps are fully usable for mail order.) I am grateful for the gift of one copy, and I hereby acknowledge it.

Little Western Heaven

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 20: Striving for Life, Watching Grandchildren, Crying and Remembering the Past, Planting Wheat and Inviting Disaster

The life of the poor is something that people with food cannot know. Naturally, the illness of the poor is something that people with food cannot understand. Li Shilian saw that Yueying's grandmother had fainted, and thought it was a terminal illness, which was greatly related to himself. The poor will do anything to get money. His family would definitely say that he had murdered her, so he should slip away before anyone from his family came out. This thought reminded him, and he immediately retracted his body and walked towards Little Western Heaven. His heart was also constantly thinking, "I'm here to visit relatives and ask about illnesses for someone's concubine, and now that I know the news, I naturally have to report it." However, if I really tell the truth, I'm afraid Yueying will cry, and he will want to go back even more. Secondly, I'm afraid he will blame me for not saving him when someone fainted at the door, and instead ran in. This question is not easy to answer. The more I thought about it, the more I felt it was right, and the slower the pace of walking became. When I was about to reach the house in front, he suddenly stopped and stood in the corner of the house, just staring blankly. Later, a waiter passed by him. Seeing him standing on the road, seemingly contemplating a trivial matter, he went in and said, "Eh! Mr. Li, did you lose something? What are you thinking about?"

Rice Market Conditions Firm, Indica Rice Improves / Report of Food Shipment to Italy Awaits Confirmation

Yesterday in the South Market, the various sources of rice still arrived at about thirty-seven or thirty-eight (with a total of over seven thousand shih (石, a unit of dry measure)) and sales were balanced. There were no changes and no significant ups or downs in the wholesale prices. The low-grade japonica rice, with about seven or eight hundred packages from Yantai and Qingdao suppliers, maintained its original price. New goods like Baige (百哥) and kiln-grown rice also continued to receive over three hundred packages. Although the weather was sunny, the market remained stable. The supply and demand for both new Du Yangjian (杜洋尖) were harmonious and without any significant changes. Old rice was traded at an ordinary price. As for Changbang (常帮) rice, the southwest new rice was already on the market yesterday. The quality of the rice was considered good and plump, but it was said that the harvest this year was affected due to the abundant rainfall, yielding only about 70% of a normal harvest. The quantity of rice arriving on the market this time was not large, and it was sold at a premium of ten yuan and one dime (角, a tenth of a yuan) because it was the first batch of fresh rice.

Thirty-seven or thirty-eight sources of rice arrived in the North Market from the river. The market was weak in the early morning, with prices falling by one or two dimes. Later, due to news of firmer prices in the production areas, buyers disregarded the taxes and actively purchased, causing the white broken rice to recover slightly, rising by several fractions of a dime to nearly a dime. Dongxin (東新) japonica rice and Xinxin (西新) japonica rice rose by one or two dimes. The closing prices had already stabilized. Xin Yangjian (新羊尖) rice was stable, Xin Dufu Jian (新杜埠尖) rice was slightly under a dime, Baiyuan (白元) rice was weak, and Xin Kejian (新客尖) rice was slightly soft. Bo Dao (薄稻) rice rose by two dimes, and Shen Ding (審　) Baige (百哥) rice rose by two or three dimes. Other goods also saw an upward trend.

The rice market was firm. Small broken rice continued to be popular due to demand from local merchants, and prices continued to rise slightly. However, Saigon rice remained stable. There was talk of a transaction involving one thousand tons the day before. Because Italy and Abyssinia had started the war, there were rumors that the price in the production area would rise. As a result, merchants in the market held back their goods and did not sell. Yesterday, only one thousand packages of small broken rice and over two hundred packages of Saigon rice were sold, all through local merchants.

The supply of Indica rice was still active, with rice from Ningbo (甬江) being the most abundant. Rice from Jiangxi, Nanjing, Anqing, and Tingbei (汀北) also continued to arrive. The newly arrived rice was all purchased by local merchants. There was still a tendency for prices to rise in the future market. Due to excessive price increases the day before, Jianghu white rice (江湖白米) recovered by one dime yesterday. Other rice varieties also rose slightly by a few fractions of a dime. Throughout the day, three hundred and thirty-nine packages of Jiangxi machine-milled early rice, one thousand two hundred and forty-six packages of Ningbo rice, three hundred and five packages of Jingxian rice, three hundred and thirty packages of Anqing rice, and two hundred packages of Jiangbei rice were all purchased by local merchants.

Following the outbreak of the war between Italy and Abyssinia, it was rumored yesterday that one hundred tons of food would be shipped to Italy on the Italian ship "Controtto" (康脫羅號). According to this newspaper's sources, it seems that about one hundred tons of food is intended to be loaded on the "Controfanin" (康脫范因號), which is scheduled to depart on the ninth of the month. It is rumored that the ship is carrying a large amount of cargo, and whether it will be able to depart and whether it will actually go to Italy remains to be confirmed.
